26b1(rnying rgyud): du ston pa tshom bu/ rnam grangs byung chags su ston pa dkyil 'khor ro// yang na rigs 'gyur kyang ye shes mi 'gyur ba tshom za/ rags dang ye shes gnyis ka 'gyur ba dkyipa 'khor ro// zhes gsungs pa rnams kyang phyogs de nas gzhag tu ba tu med bya/ 'os

26b3(rnying rgyud): sogs rigs bzhi'i gtso bo rdo rje'i rigs gcig gis bsdus pas rigs tha dad kyi gtso bo gcig tu gyur pa'i phyir dang / tshom bu ni rang gi rigs chung gis bye brag tu bskor bas rigs tha mi dad kyi gtso bo so sos byed pa'i phyir ro// 'o na rang gi rigs chung gis bye brag tu bskor

27b3(rnying rgyud): chen mi dbye bar rol/ zhes gong ma rnams gsungs/ 'grel chung las/ zhi rgyas las/ dbye ba'am dbang drag mi dbye bar/ zhes las bzhi'i gzungs ma'i khyad par du bshad/ don la sgrub pa dang phrin las kyi gzungs ma ji ltar bshad pa ltar rigs dbye ba'am/

28b7(rnying rgyud): khang nang mar slob dpon gyi drung du khrid nas las 'phrin gdags/ slob dpon gyis lan btab/ bi shwa'i sngags kyis bgegs bskrad/ bsgral bya'i spyi bor ngan song sbyor ba'i lha bskyed/ de'i sngags kyis btab pa'i yungs kar gyis spyi bo nas mar grabs pas sgrib
29a1(rnying rgyud): spangs/ thA ga pa ti'i sngags kyis 'gro drug tu rgyab skad gagag/ gnyis pa bsngal pa dngas la/ skye ba'i chun gcad pa/ dbyung ba'i klu dgag pa/ shes pa ches nying du dang / yum gyi mkhang pa dang / dzA rje sems dpang mtshan

31a1(rnying rgyud): bzug na 'bras bu da ltar 'byung ba bden kyang 'dir thabs kyis zin pa phyir ci 'gal te/ snga ma las/ khe dregs sdod pas de min te// thabs men lam la gnas pa ya/ skyes bu kun gyis bya bar gsungs// zhes so// mdor na/

249a1(rnying rgyud): pa'i// thams cad mthun pa can nas spyan// chos dbying sa ma ma ba // mnyam spyad mas shA / bya ba tha la gas pas nan ga/ dasngags ma sgrub dgasas mad cad// thang rgyab sas rgya

277a3(rnying rgyud): sngags phyag rgyas rnam par spel// rin chen rigs tshogs thams cad kyi// byin rlabs yon tan kun bsdus te// gnas lnga dag tu sbyor byas pas// thams cad rab tu rdzogs par 'gyur// 'khor los sgyur rgyal gnas chen 'grub// yang dag
277a4(rnying rgyud): sangs rgyas kun dang mnyam// tshe dbang byin rlabs nyams pa dag/ mtha' yas mgon po dpag mod sgra// mdzod su rin chen gzhal yas su// byang chub sems nyid u sha'i gzugs// 'od gsal kho dog lnga dang ldan// rigs kyi phyag rgyas
277a5(rnying rgyud): brtan byas te// chags pa'i yul bcas dbang gi sras// khro bo mtshon cha'i phreng bar bcas// yang dag sung bas bsrang byas te// mi mthun las kun rnam par ngo mas// khro bo'i sprul pa bsam yas dang // phyag rgya'i mtshan ma thams cad kyis//
277a6(rnying rgyud): yul kun gnas bcas bshig byas te// mkha' mdzod dra ba'i las chen po// rnam par spel bar rgyas pa dgra/ sangs rgyas can gyi mdangs ldan pa'o// sprul pa'i phreng ba'o dadang btsas// bkra shis g.yung drung dpal be'u mchog/ bum pa
277a7(rnying rgyud): bzang dang gzugs kyi mtshan// mi shinas nan snying po sra// phyag rgya'i bkod pa mthi' yas shing // tsho tshogs can byas mdzad // phyogs ldan pa srang bablon med// yid bzhin nor ba zan pa'i mchog/ 'dod gnas ma rnams dang /
277b1(rnying rgyud): dkyil 'khor 'bral bas chags pa'i gnas// bza' btung longs spyod thams cad la// skra gsung thugs kyis bon gyis// 'gro 'du byin rlabs sprul pa'i chags// gnas sun nya bar bskur byed cing // 'dod pa'i longs spyod rtsa mor bcas//
277b2(rnying rgyud): sangs rgyas theg pa kun gyi bdag/ dbyings dang ye shes mnyam sbyor zhing // lnga gnyis rdzogs pa'i 'od zer dang // nyi shu rtsa lnga'i 'od zer gyis// don kun gsang ba'i bdag po las// sbyor ba'i yan lag bdun du sdang // gnyis med gnyis su
277b3(rnying rgyud): 'phrul pa yi// rgyal ba kun 'byung bdag nyid do// kun tu bsrung ba'i phyag rgya yis// gnas rnams kun tu rgyas gdab cing // cod pan phreng ba myu gur bcas// rang gi dam tshig rdzogs pa'i mchog/ gnas zug sna tshogs rdo rje las// khro bo
277b4(rnying rgyud): yab yum sbyor ba'i rgya// rin chen phreng ba rdo rjes mtshan// rgyu mdud gnas kun brtan pa nyid// dbu rgyan rigs lnga'i mtshan mas mdzes// sangs rgyas kun rdzogs dbang bskur mchog/ sna tshogs ba dan phreng sogs bklubs// grong khyer bzang po'i
277b5(rnying rgyud): gnas 'di ru// bsod nams ye shes tshogs rdzogs pa'i// lha mo'i mchod pa bla na med// thubs la shes rab rol pa dang // thabs kyis shes rab rol pa nyid// 'jug pa rgyu dang 'bras bu mchog/ bya ba rdzogs pa'i phyag rgya yis/ yang
277b6(rnying rgyud): dag 'pho ba brten mdzad cing // phyogs mtshams gnas kun 'jug pa'i tshul// mi gnyis rdo rje'i tshig ldan pas// glu gar dbyangs kyis kun bskyod cing // yan lag rol pa'i 'khor lo dag/ rnam par sbyang ba'i byang chub sems// mtshan ldan pad+ma'i pho
277b7(rnying rgyud): brang drud// bdud rtsi rnam pa lnga dang bcas// byin rlabs 'grubs pas gsal ba nyid// 'de'i chen po'i ginas rnams su// rol pa brtul zhugs gar bskur zhing // lha mo'i tshogs kyi gar dang dbyings// sprul pa'i don kun spyod pa'i mchogab
278a1(rnying rgyud): nams tshogs kyi 'khor lo yis// lus dag chung bcas dag 'gyur zhing // rnam grol dkyil 'khor rdzogs pa'i mchog/ ye shes tshogs mchog mtha' yas pa'o// kun tu smon lam ma 'gags pas// mthan
278a2(rnying rgyud): ma'i yul kun sbyor byed kyang // zag bcas spyad pa'i rtog las byung // khams gsum 'bras bu las dang bcas// thugs rje ye shes byin rlabs mthus// gnyis med dngos grub 'bras bu rnams// yul kun rdzogs pa'i stobs kyis ni// zag pa
278a3(rnying rgyud): med pa'i bde 'byung zhing // rang gi ngo bo gsal bar byed// spyod pa rnam par grol ba'i mchog/ rgyal ba'i mdzad pa kun rdzogs pa'o// rdo rje sems dpa' sgyu 'phrul dra ba gsang ba'i snying po de kho na nyid ngol pa chen po'i chud las/ spyod pa bstan pa'i le'u ste brgya
278a4(rnying rgyud): gnyis pa'o// // de nas 'khor gyi tshogs rnams yis// sangs rgyas kun gyi dkyil 'khor la// rab tu brtags pas 'jug gyur cing // byin rlabs yul kun rnam par 'jug/ rang gi ye shes ji lta bar// de dag sdang po bsam mi khyab//
278a5(rnying rgyud): chos kyi rgyun gyi bya ba dag/ mngon par sna pas rgyu chen rdzogs// ngo mtshur ya mtshan gnas la 'jug/ sangs rgyas thams cad bstan pa'i gnas// rnam par sbas pas gas ba'i tshul// phyag tu thabs tshogs chog kun// bstan pa'i gnas su 'byung
278a6(rnying rgyud): sa nan sa
278a7(rnying rgyud): 'khor kun 'jug cing // sum cu rtse gnyis rdzogs pa ye// bsnyen pasgrub yan lag gnas chen po// a ta a sha'i spyod ldan pas// 'jigs byed ya ta tsata'i mtha'// pho brang ma bcos pad+ma'i dbyings// btab ngas dang / rtswa yi 'jug
278b1(rnying rgyud): pa rnam bdun gyis// rkyen gyi nam mkha' rnam par dag/ yang dag nye bar bsags pa'i rgyun// jug dang drug bcas mtha' rnams 'gog/ 'bras bu deng gnas mthun pa'i chos// rnam gsum sbyor ba'i stobs kyis rdzogs// nywamang mang du
278b2(rnying rgyud): thabs rnams kyis// rgyal ba'i pho brang bcu drug gnas// zla phyed yongs su rdzogs pa yi// dkyil 'khor gsal ba ched rgyas 'gyur// mtshan ma sna tshogs ting 'dzin dngos// de dag gnas kun lhun grub pa'i// rigs kyi yi ge bzang po'i
278b3(rnying rgyud): tshogs// mtshan ma med pa'i ting 'dzin mchog/ sangs rgyas theg pa mdor bsdus te// yul dang yul can gnyis med par// byang chub sems bsags cha rgyas pas// rang bzhin rnam dag dkyil 'khor mchog/ mi rtog ngo bo dbyibs dang
278b4(rnying rgyud): bral// rab sbyangs spyod pas rdzogs 'gyur zhing // pho brang yi ge'i cha bral ba// yul kun sbyangs pa'i ting 'dzin ni// dkyil 'khor bdag dang gzhan pa'i rgyud// kun nas sgyu 'phrul dra ba'i dngos// tha dad yul gnyis bsam yas pa'i// phreng
278b5(rnying rgyud): baM cha dang cha las 'das// dmigs pa kun nas 'jug pa'i rgyun// de mtha' spos dang bsdu ba'i tshul// mnyam nyid rtogs pa rnam lnga yi// phyag rgya rdzogs pa thig le'i tshul// rang gi gnas 'jug thig le'i chu// 'khor lo'i tshul bzhin 'jug pa'o//
278b6(rnying rgyud): ji srid dngos grub snying po mchog/ rab tu rtogs pa rnam bzhi yis// bye brag yul tshogs gnyis med par // snang ba rnam par dag pa'i tshul// nye bar bsdus pas rdzas byas te// dam tshig dkyil 'khor mnyam ldan pa// thugs rje 'byung ba'i bdag
278b7(rnying rgyud): po nyid// ye shes sems dpa' sngags lam las// dam tshig 'phro 'du'i bye brag gis// yan lag gnas kun rdzogs 'gyung zhing // 'od kyi thig le rnam par dag/ bu ga'i tshogs rnams thams cad dang // dbang po dug gi gnas khyab cing //
279a1(rnying rgyud): rten dang brten pa'i ye shes tshogs// ting 'dzin sems dpa' bdag nyid do// sa bon zla ba theg ler bcas// yang dag sbyangs pas rdzogs pa'i sgra// byang chub gnas kyi rgyan ldan zhing // mthar phyin sangs rgyas
279a2(rnying rgyud): kun gyi thugs// dus gsum rgyun gyi ting nge 'dzin// ngo bo gcig nyid sna tshogs mdangs// thabs kyi 'bul ba mtha' yas te// sangs rgyas drug gi mdzad bcas pas// dkyil 'khor bla na med pa'i mchog/ ye shes dkyil 'khor thams can kun/
279a3(rnying rgyud): dga' mgri dngus pas mnyes byas tAM// 'khor lo cha shas gnyis kyi tshul// gsol 'dabs grags dang phyag tu yis// rang gi yul dugashegs gsol zhing // dus ring 'gro la gzigs pa'i mthus// ji srid bkod pa na ched ngon// pha rol phyin pa'i
279a4(rnying rgyud): tshogs rnams kyi// sangs rgyas theg pa bstan par byed// sbyin sogs tshul khrims bzod pa dang // brtson 'grus bsam gtan shes rab sogs// brags stobs smon lam ye shes kyi// bya ba chen pos gzhan chung sel// yang dag mnyam nyid ye shes che//
279a5(rnying rgyud): 'gro rnams rdo rje 'dzin pa'o// gnas kun mngon par sbyor byas te// thabs dang shes rab sbyor ba'i bdag/ gnyis med 'phrul pas bsam yas pa// de dag rnam par rdzogs pa yi// byang chub yan lag rin chen rdzas// rang gi gnas dang gnas med

279b5(rnying rgyud): thugs// ye shes rgya mtsho dpag med kyi// yon tan rdzogs pa'i ngo bor gnas// 'og min chen po'i gzhal yas khang // rgyal ba kun gyi b+ha ga'i gnas// yon tan kun rdzogs dga' ba'i klong // tshad med ye shes chos dbyings kyi//
279b6(rnying rgyud): ngo bos kun nas 'khyil ba la// tshang dpag med pa'i yon tan rgyas// rnam thar bzhi yi sgo khyud mdzes// 'dod yon lnga yi phreng bas brgyan// rnam thar bkyad kyi rta babs can// zla ba'i phreng bas mdangs phyung zhing // nyi zla pad+ma'i gdan steng na/
